NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

[Part VI—Sec. 4

NOTICES
PUBLIC NOTICE
I, K. Manuvel, born as an intersexed male child to Mr. M. Kuppusamy on 25th May 1985, residing at No. 2/57, Poothanur,
Konagapadi Post, Omalur Taluk, Salem, after Biological change, has been reared as a Female. (Reference:
Dr. S.A.K. Meeran, M.S. (Gen.), Senior Surgical Consultant, Reg. No. 17952, Madurai Surgical Hospital, Dindigul-1)
The Clinical Examination under the reference above also show that I could be reared as a Female. Hence I, K. Manuvel shall
henceforth be known as K. INDHU.
Salem, 30th April 2010.

K. MANUVEL.
